### Simultaneous Substitution

### Reflexive and transitive closure

### Lookup 

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="9553" class="Keyword">data</a> <a id="Problem3._∋_⦂_"></a><a id="9558" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Exam.md %}{% raw %}#9558" class="Datatype Operator">_∋_⦂_</a> <a id="9564" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9566" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Exam.md %}{% raw %}#8874" class="Datatype">Context</a> <a id="9574" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="9576" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Exam.md %}{% raw %}#8805" class="Function">Id</a> <a id="9579" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="9581" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Exam.md %}{% raw %}#8695" class="Datatype">Type</a> <a id="9586" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="9588" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a> <a id="9592" class="Keyword">where</a>

    <a id="Problem3._∋_⦂_.Z"></a><a id="9603" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Exam.md %}{% raw %}#9603" class="InductiveConstructor">Z</a> <a id="9605" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9607" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="9609" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="9610" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Exam.md %}{% raw %}#9610" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="9612" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Exam.md %}{% raw %}#9612" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="9614" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Exam.md %}{% raw %}#9614" class="Bound">A</a><a id="9615" class="Symbol">}</a>
        <a id="9625" class="Comment">--------------------</a>
      <a id="9652" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="9654" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Exam.md %}{% raw %}#9610" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="9656" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Exam.md %}{% raw %}#8918" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="9658" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Exam.md %}{% raw %}#9612" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="9660" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Exam.md %}{% raw %}#8918" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⦂</a> <a id="9662" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Exam.md %}{% raw %}#9614" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="9664" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Exam.md %}{% raw %}#9558" class="Datatype Operator">∋</a> <a id="9666" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Exam.md %}{% raw %}#9612" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="9668" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Exam.md %}{% raw %}#9558" class="Datatype Operator">⦂</a> <a id="9670" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Exam.md %}{% raw %}#9614" class="Bound">A</a>
